466、Some days the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/sunsets">sunsets</a> would be <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/purple">purple</a> and <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/pink">pink</a>. And some days they were a <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/blazing">blazing</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/orange">orange</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/setting">setting</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/fire">fire</a> to the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/clouds">clouds</a> on the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/horizon">horizon</a>. It was <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/during">during</a> one of those <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/sunsets">sunsets</a> that my father's <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/idea">idea</a> of the whole being <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/greater">greater</a> than the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/sum">sum</a> of its <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/parts">parts</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/moved">moved</a> from my <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/head">head</a> to my heart.   有时，落日泛起紫红的余晖，有时，散发出橘红色的火光，燃起天边的晚霞。在这绚烂的日落景象中，我慢慢领悟了父亲所说的整体胜于局部总和的道理。—影片《怦然心动》<br/>
467、I think people just get <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/frustrated">frustrated</a> without how <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/harsh">harsh</a> life can be, so they're <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/spending">spending</a> their time <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/dwelling">dwelling</a> on that <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/frustration">frustration</a> – we <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/calling">calling</a> it <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/anger">anger</a> – <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/keeping">keeping</a> their eyes <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/shut">shut</a> to the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/wholeness">wholeness</a> of the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/situation">situation</a>, to all those little, <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/tinny">tinny</a> things that have come together to make it.   我想，人们在不知生活会有多困苦时就感到失败，所以人们便久久围困于自己的失败中，我们称之为愤怒——对这一局面的整体视而不见，也对那些造成这种局面的各种细小的、琐碎的细节视而不见。—影片《风雨哈佛路》<br/>
468、And, in an ordinary <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/barn">barn</a>, an ordinary <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/pig">pig</a>, a <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/runt">runt</a> no less, <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/stood">stood</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/surrounded">surrounded</a> by friends, <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/welcoming">welcoming</a> his second spring. And that spring was <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/followed">followed</a> by many, many more – all because someone <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/stopped">stopped</a> to see the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/grace">grace</a> and beauty and <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/nobility">nobility</a> of the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/humblest">humblest</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/creature">creature</a>. That is the miracle of <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/friendship">friendship</a>.   在一个很平常的谷仓里，一只平常的猪，依旧还是个猪崽，被他的朋友包围着，迎接他生命里第二个春天的到来，当然，他还要迎接更多更多的春天，而这全都是因为有人为他停下来，用心记录了这个最谦卑生命的优雅、美丽和高贵之处——这是关于友情的奇迹。—影片《夏洛特的网》<br/>
